class="cl-9062e9d8">The report, issued in May 1947, called for an end to external assistance to Greek Communist guerrillas.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9063242a"><p class="cl-9062f608"><span activity, was vetoed by the USSR.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90632448"><p class="cl-9062f608"><span class="cl-9062e9ec">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9062e9ec"> </span><span 1948.</span></p></td><td class="cl-909f0de7"><p class="cl-909edc0e"><span class="cl-909ed06a">No</span><span class="cl-909ed06a"> </span><span class="cl-909ed06a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr with the Soviet NKVD. class="cl-90e9c43a">Indonesia responded on 25 December by setting up an emergency government in Sumatra and appealing to Prime Minister Nehru of India, who transmitted to the Security Council the resolution adopted by the second New Delhi Conference on Indonesia, with strong recommendations for action.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Indonesia</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">initiated</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">institutions</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">change</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">toward</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">.</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Indonesia</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">initiated</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">institutions</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">change</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f702"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.9</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">The Netherlands responded on the 27th by rejecting the Security Council's call for an immediate cease-fire and the transfer of sovereignty to Indonesia after free elections.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">initiated</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">reject</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">toward</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"><br></span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">United</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Nations</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f70c"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.10</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">On the 30th it refused to accept the cease-fire and release political prisoners.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">initiated</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">reject</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">toward</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"><br></span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">United</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Nations;Indonesia</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f702"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.11</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">The UN formed the United Nations Commission for Indonesia, which included representatives from Australia, Belgium and the United States, to assist in the resolution process.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c44e">United</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Nations</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">initiated</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">mediation</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">toward</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Indonesia;Netherlands</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f70c"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.12</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">At a meeting on 14 April 1949, the U.S. representative, H. Merle Cochran, proposed 17 points to be considered at a round table discussion between the UNCI and the belligerent actors, held from 23 August to 2 November 1949.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">No</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f702"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.13</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">Additional international pressure -- from the second New Delhi Conference, an Arab League resolution calling for a Dutch cease-fire, and intense U.S. pressure -- finally convinced the Netherlands to comply.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">No</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f70c"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.14</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">The crisis ended for both actors on 27 December 1949, when Queen Juliana signed a formal act transferring sovereignty over the Dutch East Indies to the Republic of Indonesia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f703"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">experienced</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">a</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">end</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">of</span><span class="cl-90e9c44e"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">crisis</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">.</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Netherlands</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">initiated</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">toward</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c44e">Indonesia</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f702"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.15</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">The Soviet Union supported Indonesia politically throughout its conflict with the Netherlands, 1945-49.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f6f8"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">No</span><span class="cl-90e9c43a"> </span><span class="cl-90e9c43a">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-90e9f70d"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">127.16</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f70e"><p class="cl-90e9cfa2"><span class="cl-90e9c43a">The U.S., on the other hand, changed from supporting the Netherlands to pressing them to sign the Renville Agreement, to securing Dutch compliance with UN resolutions by threatening to suspend U.S. aid.</span></p></td><td class="cl-90e9f70e"><p
